  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_f010b059-424e-4a19-99ad-90f04df4fa5e'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<span id="freeTextContainer18230869701649767128">Two years before Beatrice Prior made her choice, the sixteen-year-old son of Abnegation’s faction leader did the same. Tobias’s transfer to Dauntless is a chance to begin again. Here, he will not be called the name his parents gave him. Here, he will not let fear turn him into a cowering child.<br/><br/>Newly christened “Four,” he discovers during initiation that he will succeed in </span>
  <span id="freeText18230869701649767128" style="display:none">Two years before Beatrice Prior made her choice, the sixteen-year-old son of Abnegation’s faction leader did the same. Tobias’s transfer to Dauntless is a chance to begin again. Here, he will not be called the name his parents gave him. Here, he will not let fear turn him into a cowering child.<br /><br />Newly christened “Four,” he discovers during initiation that he will succeed in Dauntless. Initiation is only the beginning, though; Four must claim his place in the Dauntless hierarchy. His decisions will affect future initiates as well as uncover secrets that could threaten his own future—and the future of the entire faction system.<br /><br />Two years later, Four is poised to take action, but the course is still unclear. The first new initiate who jumps into the net might change all that. With her, the way to righting their world might become clear. With her, it might become possible to be Tobias once again.<br /><br />From #1 <i>New York Times</i> bestselling author Veronica Roth comes a companion volume to the worldwide bestselling DIVERGENT series, told from the per-spective of the immensely popular character Tobias. The four pieces included here—THE TRANSFER, THE INITIATE, THE SON, and THE TRAITOR—plus three additional exclusive scenes, give readers an electrifying glimpse into the history and heart of Tobias, and set the stage for the epic saga of the DIVERGENT trilogy.</span>

It is very similar to DIVERGENT in both writing style and plot development. To me<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">The state of this book being "good" depends on your personal tastes. It is very similar to DIVERGENT in both writing style and plot development. To me personally, the stories felt a bit unnecessary because of how similar they were to Tris's initiation and such, but if you're a hardcore fan of the series and you love Four, it's a fun read.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

<div id="review_2345686286" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2345686286" />
    <a title="Miranda Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/71848701-miranda-reads"><img alt="Miranda Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1592243041p2/71848701.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2345686286?book_show_action=true">Apr 02, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Miranda Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Miranda Reads" href="/user/show/71848701-miranda-reads">Miranda Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/71848701-miranda-reads?shelf=2018-abc-reading-challenge">2018-abc-reading-challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/71848701-miranda-reads?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/71848701-miranda-reads?shelf=dumpster-fire">dumpster-fire</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/71848701-miranda-reads?shelf=literally-painful-to-read">literally-painful-to-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/71848701-miranda-reads?shelf=ya-series">ya-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2345686286" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer723304723059924832"><b>Overwhelmingly underwhelming.</b><br/><br/>And that is as about as positive as I can get.<br/><br/>It felt more like the author was<b> frantically filling in plot holes</b> rather than writing something new. <br/><br/><b>
  <u>The Transfer</u>
</b> - Was this one <b>
  <i>reallllly</i>
</b> necessary??? <br/><br/>From the main books, <b>we already know </b>that Four picked Dauntless because he wanted to escape his abusive father.<br/><br/> And this short story....<b>told exactly that.</b> I suppose, it was just a really, really drawn out version... but still. <b>Felt like a waste of page space. </b><br/><br/><u>
  <b>T</b></u></span>
  <span id="freeText723304723059924832" style="display:none"><b>Overwhelmingly underwhelming.</b><br /><br />And that is as about as positive as I can get.<br /><br />It felt more like the author was<b> frantically filling in plot holes</b> rather than writing something new. <br /><br /><b>
  <u>The Transfer</u>
</b> - Was this one <b>
  <i>reallllly</i>
</b> necessary??? <br /><br />From the main books, <b>we already know </b>that Four picked Dauntless because he wanted to escape his abusive father.<br /><br /> And this short story....<b>told exactly that.</b> I suppose, it was just a really, really drawn out version... but still. <b>Felt like a waste of page space. </b><br /><br /><u>
  <b>The Initiate</b>
</u> - This was a<b>
  <i> bit </i>
</b>interesting. <br /><br />We see some of the main players from Divergent (mainly Eric and the Dauntless-born initiates) as <b>Four comes to terms with his new life. </b><br /><br />But honestly, it feels like we already lived through this. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>Divergent</i>
</b> - A Stiff enters dauntless, gets ridiculed but manages to come out on top.<br /><br /><i>
  <b> The Initiate </b>
</i>- A Stiff enters dauntless <b>BUT he's like, super nervous and stuff</b>, gets ridiculed and manages to come out on top. <br /><br /> And we see how he gets his tat. That bit <b>bugged the ever-living daylights out of me</b>.<br /><br /> He goes on and on about how NO ONE CAN KNOW HE'S DIVERGENT. And what does he do? <b>Literally gets <u>the most divergent possible tattoo</u> on his body ever.</b> I mean, honestly. This kid.<br /><br /><b> <u>The Son</u> </b> - Four trains for a leadership position.<br /><br /> He spends most of the time waffling on whether or not he wants to do it. Then decides not to <b>"because reasons."</b> <br /><br />Four is all like, "oh no, I don't like that my faction is corrupted. Whine whine whine." <br /><br />Then he abandons the leadership position thus allowing the corrupted guy to get the spot. <b> NO WONDER YOUR FACTION FALLS APART.</b><br /><br /><b>
  <u>The Traitor</u>
</b> - honestly just filling in plot holes.<br /><br />How does he get into the computer room?<br /><br /> How does he know about the abnegation attack? <br /><br />Then, he meets Tris and falls in love with her because reasons. <b>Blah blah blah. </b><br /><br /><b>
  <u>Extra scenes from Four's perspective</u>
</b> - talk about a waste of paper. No inner revelations, no big reveals. <br /><br />Honestly, I think I preferred it when we weren't in his head.<b> He seemed much more interesting that way. </b><br /><br /><i> The Finer Books Club 2018 Reading Challenge - a book with a number in the title</i><br /><br /><a href="http://bit.ly/33ii2CT" rel="nofollow noopener">YouTube</a> | <a href="http://www.mirandareads.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/miranda.reads/?hl=en" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/Miranda_Reads" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | Snapchat @miranda.reads <br /><br />Happy Reading!</span>
  <a data-text-id="723304723059924832" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1182993003" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1182993003" />
    <a title="Ida" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23173697-ida"><img alt="Ida" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1423853357p2/23173697.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1182993003?book_show_action=true">Oct 15, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ida" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ida" href="/user/show/23173697-ida">Ida</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22021811-four">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1182993003" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15637478732393208508">Oh how I've missed the Divergent universe and all of its characters!<br/><br/><blockquote> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1511007544ra/24475922.gif' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> </blockquote><br/><br/>Four, Tris, Zeke, Shauna, Uriaha, Christina, Marlene and Lynn. If it's one thing Veronica Roth is the master of, it's creating realistic and likeable characters that you'll end up caring for. <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ ..and then ripping them away one by one!  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1511007072ra/24475860.gif' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Four: A Divergent Collection includes four short stories, all told from Tobias POV, and three exclusive scenes from Divergent.<br/><br/>The short stories:<br/><br/><b> Four: The Transer </b></span>
  <span id="freeText15637478732393208508" style="display:none">Oh how I've missed the Divergent universe and all of its characters!<br><br><blockquote> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1511007544ra/24475922.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </blockquote><br><br>Four, Tris, Zeke, Shauna, Uriaha, Christina, Marlene and Lynn. If it's one thing Veronica Roth is the master of, it's creating realistic and likeable characters that you'll end up caring for. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ ..and then ripping them away one by one!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1511007072ra/24475860.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Four: A Divergent Collection includes four short stories, all told from Tobias POV, and three exclusive scenes from Divergent.<br><br>The short stories:<br><br><b> Four: The Transer </b> ⭐⭐⭐⭐ You can read my full review: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1182993013?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a><br>The transfer follows Tobias from the day of his aptitude test, though his Choosing day and until the moment he's given his infamous nickname- Four. It gives you a better understanding of the choice he made, and why he chose dauntless as apposed to any of the other factions. <br><br><b> Four: The Initiate </b> ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐ You can read my full review: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1182993125?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a><br>The Initiate follows Four through a series of events, like his first time drinking, getting his first tattoo, making friends, training and fighting. You also get more insight in some of the characters that appear in the Divergent series, like Amar, Zeke and Shauna. <br><br><b> Four: The Son </b> ⭐⭐⭐⭐ You can read my full review: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2135834466?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a><br>The Son follows Four as he struggles to find his place in the hierarchy of Dauntless. We see him train for a leadership position mentioned in Divergent, and why he really made the choice of becoming an instructor instead. <br><br><b> Four: The Traitor </b> ⭐⭐⭐⭐ You can read my full review: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2135834482?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a><br>The Traitor follows Tobias as he struggles with revelations from the previous stories, as well as some new information, while he's getting to know Tris Prior. <br><br>The exclusive scenes:<br><br><b> First jumper - Tris </b><br>I´m so happy Veronica included this in the book, as it's one of the scenes I really wanted to read from Fours POV. <br><br><blockquote> <i> This way, they’ll remember her, not for the gray she wears but for her first act of bravery. Or insanity. Sometimes they’re the same thing. </i> </blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1511007438ra/24475888.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> Careful, Tris </b><br><br><blockquote> <i> “Were you a transfer too?” <br>“I thought I would only have trouble with the Candor asking too many questions,” I say. “Now I’ve got Stiffs, too?” <br>“It must be because you’re so approachable. You know. Like a bed of nails.” <br>“Careful, Tris,” </i> </blockquote><br><br><b> You look good, Tris </b><br><br><blockquote> <i> “You look good, Tris,” I say, because I’m not sure she knows it, and she should.<br><br>One thing I know: For helping me forget how awful the world is, I prefer her to alcohol. </i> </blockquote><br><br>If you're a fan of Divergent, you'll probably like this book. If you're not a fan, then you'll probably find it unnecessary as it doesn't really offer any new information. <br>If you haven't read Divergent yet, just do it! They are <b>AMAZING</b> and so emotional!</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_2072348687" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2072348687" />
    <a title="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/69106439-virginia-ronan-herondale"><img alt="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577855357p2/69106439.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2072348687?book_show_action=true">Apr 02, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" href="/user/show/69106439-virginia-ronan-herondale">Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780007550142" href="/book/show/18606526-four">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69106439-virginia-ronan-herondale?shelf=science-fiction">science-fiction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2072348687" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4905337847684753142"><i>”I don’t care what she says – this isn’t a safe room. There are no safe rooms, no safe truths, no safe secrets to tell.”</i><br/><br/>I was always intrigued by Four and his history before he became a Dauntless, so when I found this little gem in the YA section of my library I actually let out a little squeal. Apparently it was loud enough to cause a few raised eyebrows and disapproving looks, but hey this girl here just couldn’t contain herself. XD In my defence: It’s rare to find a book you wanted to read fo</span>
  <span id="freeText4905337847684753142" style="display:none"><i>”I don’t care what she says – this isn’t a safe room. There are no safe rooms, no safe truths, no safe secrets to tell.”</i><br /><br />I was always intrigued by Four and his history before he became a Dauntless, so when I found this little gem in the YA section of my library I actually let out a little squeal. Apparently it was loud enough to cause a few raised eyebrows and disapproving looks, but hey this girl here just couldn’t contain herself. XD In my defence: It’s rare to find a book you wanted to read for ages and I certainly didn’t expect my library to actually have it. *lol*<br /><br />Well anyway, I loved <b>“Divergent”</b> and even though the series lost its appeal during the second book I’m still a huge fan of Tobias and Tris. =) Of course I immediately borrowed the book! ;-P<br /><br /><i>”I wince as his fingers stabilize my head, and hope he doesn’t see it, doesn’t see how even his slightest touch terrifies me.”</i><br /><br />I really liked those additional stories from Four’s POV and the only reason I gave it a 3 star rating (I really would need half stars here because it would actually be 3,5) is the simple fact that not a lot is happening. I suppose this was to be expected because it are merely four (haha Four) short stories that give us a better insight at Tobias life before Divergent truly happened. <br /><br /><i>”I struggle for air, but it’s not because of my aching legs; it’s because of my weak heart, growing stronger with each passing second.”</i><br /><br />Still, those stories were interesting to read and kind of caused me to remember why I loved the first book so much! XD Poor Tobias though. He’s such a broken boy and to read about his struggle to become a part of Dauntless strongly reminded me of Tris initiation in the first book. Which might have been Veronica Roth’s intention all along but who knows? *shrugs* <br /><br /><i>”I’ve learned to be stronger, but one thing I haven’t learned, won’t let myself learn, is how to enjoy causing someone else pain. If I’m going to become Dauntless, I’m going to do it on my terms, even if that means that a part of me will always be a Stiff.”</i><br /><br />Anything else I need to tell you?<br />Yep, I almost forgot that Eric, that little numpty, was an Erudite before he transferred to Dauntless. Who would have thought it? *lol* <b>AND</b> I was surprised about Amar’s little role. I mean after reading the trilogy I really would have thought that Four and him were closer. For me this wasn’t consistent and so I was a little confused about why Tobias trusted him so much. <br /><br /><i>”I will not be molded and shaped by Jeanine Matthews. I will not be a pawn, not for them and not for my mother and not for my father; I will not belong to anyone but myself.”</i><br /><br /><b>Conclusion:</b><br />I enjoyed reading “Four” and I’m sure everyone who liked Tobias will be happy to read those stories as well. They are a nice addition to the Divergent universe and I’m glad I stumbled upon them in the library. ;-) <br />Enjoy!</span>
  <a data-text-id="4905337847684753142" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_974625138" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/974625138" />
    <a title="Roshni Ajmal" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15947368-roshni-ajmal"><img alt="Roshni Ajmal" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1438730567p2/15947368.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/974625138?book_show_action=true">Jun 22, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Roshni Ajmal" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Roshni Ajmal" href="/user/show/15947368-roshni-ajmal">Roshni Ajmal</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780062345219" href="/book/show/19501684-four">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Die Hard Divergent fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15947368-roshni-ajmal?shelf=4-stars">4-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15947368-roshni-ajmal?shelf=divergent">divergent</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15947368-roshni-ajmal?shelf=favorite-couples">favorite-couples</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15947368-roshni-ajmal?shelf=2014-favorites">2014-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15947368-roshni-ajmal?shelf=my-heart">my-heart</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer974625138" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13338494534599372430"><b>And i fell in love with Four all over again</b><br/><br/>Reading Four made me feel this weird feeling, That feeling you get when you watch your old photos or videos like. I was not prepared for this.<br/><br/>There is nothing new.... Its more like behind the scenes. We get know that what Four was up to all along. like. how he discovered about the attack on abnegation. It was good that it was not divergent all over again.<br/><br/>We get to see his friendships with Zeak, Shauna and others. and his Hateship with Eric too.<br/><br/>Four is o</span>
  <span id="freeText13338494534599372430" style="display:none"><b>And i fell in love with Four all over again</b><br><br>Reading Four made me feel this weird feeling, That feeling you get when you watch your old photos or videos like. I was not prepared for this.<br><br>There is nothing new.... Its more like behind the scenes. We get know that what Four was up to all along. like. how he discovered about the attack on abnegation. It was good that it was not divergent all over again.<br><br>We get to see his friendships with Zeak, Shauna and others. and his Hateship with Eric too.<br><br>Four is one of my favourite character of all time. (forgetting the fact that allegiant ever happened). I loved him in divergent and same for this one. I got the same old feeling of liking him. <br><br>In Allegiant Four's voice was too similar to Tris's and I disliked it. But here Four's voice sounded orignal. It really felt like it was HIM speaking. <br><br>When i read divergent i felt that i was right there in the dauntless sector. This one also has that power to make you feel you are present right there. <br><br>Last three scenes from Fours POV were the best parts of this book.<br>First Jumper—Tris<br>Careful —Tris<br>You look good—Tris<br>When i closed this book all submerged feelings of Divergent came back on the surface all over again.<br><br><b>Fav Quote :</b><br><blockquote>“One thing I know: For helping me forget how awful the world is, I prefer her to alcohol.” — Four</blockquote><br>Because it was the last line of book and i had this big giant smile on my face. <br><br>If you loved Four like i did then read it. If you didn't then leave it.<br><br>I will leave you with these gif.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408507349ra/10857728.gif" width="200" height="106" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408506182ra/10857547.gif" width="200" height="106" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408507349ra/10857729.gif" width="200" height="106" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408507349ra/10857730.gif" width="200" height="106" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408507349ra/10857731.gif" width="200" height="106" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408507349ra/10857732.gif" width="200" height="106" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408507727ra/10857777.gif" width="200" height="106" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408507727ra/10857778.gif" width="200" height="106" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>------------------<br><b>I swear i didnt wanted to read anything from Veronica Roth. But common how can i resist these quotes and our good old Four. <br>AHhhhhh<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403466146i/10096685.jpg" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403466146i/10096686.jpg" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403466146i/10096687.jpg" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403466146i/10096688.jpg" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403466498i/10096711.jpg" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403920443i/10164820.jpg" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403920860i/10164919.jpg" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403920860i/10164920.jpg" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></b></span>

<div id="review_1015287285" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1015287285" />
    <a title="karen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/45618-karen"><img alt="karen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1596291582p2/45618.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1015287285?book_show_action=true">Aug 03, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="karen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="karen" href="/user/show/45618-karen">karen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/45618-karen?shelf=thanks-for-prezzies">thanks-for-prezzies</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/45618-karen?shelf=why-yes-i-ya">why-yes-i-ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/45618-karen?shelf=hey-shorty">hey-shorty</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1015287285" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6290325000136528997">hahaha <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/867613205?book_show_action=false&page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>kelly's review</a> for this cracks me up. <br/><br/>and i totally agree with the fact that sometimes when something is over, you just have to let it be over. make a clean break. but i am, in many ways, a completist. i have seen all the movies in the <i>saw</i> franchise, i keep getting wicked excited every time i see there is a new <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/series/47749-newsflesh' rel='nofollow noopener'>newsflesh short story</a> available, just when i thought i would never get to revisit that world, and i will read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/list/45618-karen?authenticity_token=w9DEca4eELUChy12R9MrgP7FEICrsAzHi6YgmcDH97k%3D&shelf=smotherings&user_id=45618' rel='nofollow noopener'>any and all retellings of wuthering heights</a>, no matter how dreadful.<br/><br/>so</span>
  <span id="freeText6290325000136528997" style="display:none">hahaha <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/867613205?book_show_action=false&amp;page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">kelly's review</a> for this cracks me up. <br><br>and i totally agree with the fact that sometimes when something is over, you just have to let it be over. make a clean break. but i am, in many ways, a completist. i have seen all the movies in the <i>saw</i> franchise, i keep getting wicked excited every time i see there is a new <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/47749-newsflesh" rel="nofollow noopener">newsflesh short story</a> available, just when i thought i would never get to revisit that world, and i will read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/list/45618-karen?authenticity_token=w9DEca4eELUChy12R9MrgP7FEICrsAzHi6YgmcDH97k%3D&amp;shelf=smotherings&amp;user_id=45618" rel="nofollow noopener">any and all retellings of wuthering heights</a>, no matter how dreadful.<br><br>so i get the impulse that leads to the perpetuation of a series, even when it might not be "necessary" in terms of addressing unanswered questions or filling in any timelines. because this one isn't, really, except for giving fourgasms to the fangirls:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407276444ra/10667332.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398839183ra/9470440.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>i thought it was interesting when roth made the move in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18710190.Allegiant__Divergent___3_" title="Allegiant (Divergent, #3) by Veronica Roth" rel="nofollow noopener">Allegiant</a> from tris-centric narration to a tris-and-four split-narrative. it was intriguing to get another perspective to the events, and to gain insight into four's mind, rather than just seeing all of his actions through tris' eyes. and, well, obviously there was more of a structural need to give him a voice in that third book. this collection reads like a bunch of "what-if" writing exercises. what if we'd had four's voice all along? what if this scene had been seen through his eyes in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13335037.Divergent__Divergent___1_" title="Divergent (Divergent, #1) by Veronica Roth" rel="nofollow noopener">Divergent</a>? what if we knew his motivations from the very beginning? these stories end up being fun without being particularly illuminating. we get more reasons to hate eric and marcus, we get a little more texture to four's relationship with evelyn, and we get a little more uriah ♥. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407276444i/10667333.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>but honestly, part of what made four compelling as a character was his secrecy. he was enigmatic, troubled, hard to predict. his POV in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18710190.Allegiant__Divergent___3_" title="Allegiant (Divergent, #3) by Veronica Roth" rel="nofollow noopener">Allegiant</a> was compelling for the novelty of it, but it took some of his power away as a character, because his weaknesses were more exposed. sure, it was humanizing, but sometimes it's better not to know all the dopey-moony things your tall dark and handsome is thinking, yeah? <br><br>but, overall i enjoyed it - i did like the details and the dovetailing it did with the things that were already known to readers, and in the bound (non-digital) edition, there are an additional three scenes after the four <i>four</i> novellas, which is even MOAR FOUR for your buck.<br><br>thanks to greg for buying me a book about FOUR!!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1528725630i/25720315.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><a href="http://bloggycomelately.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">come to my blog!</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="6290325000136528997" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer156325640811552923"><i>“That's what I really want - to shed all the people who want to form and shape me, one by one, and learn instead to form and shape myself.”</i><br/><br/>4.5 out of 5<br/><br/>I had a great time with this collection of <i>Divergent</i> short stories. Reading about this universe from Four's POV was really fascinating. It was nice to get to see what he thought in those situations. Of course, I already knew a lot of what was going to happen so there were not too many surprises in this book. I just really loved reading scenes with</span>
  <span id="freeText156325640811552923" style="display:none"><i>“That's what I really want - to shed all the people who want to form and shape me, one by one, and learn instead to form and shape myself.”</i><br /><br />4.5 out of 5<br /><br />I had a great time with this collection of <i>Divergent</i> short stories. Reading about this universe from Four's POV was really fascinating. It was nice to get to see what he thought in those situations. Of course, I already knew a lot of what was going to happen so there were not too many surprises in this book. I just really loved reading scenes with Four and Tris in particular.<br /><br />Apart from that I can't get enough from Veronica Roth. She should consider writing faster, cause I'm desperate for more. Veronica is seriously one of the most amazing writes in YA today.<br /><br /><a href="https://www.instagram.com/fantasticbooksandwheretofindem/" rel="nofollow noopener">Find more of my books on Instagram</a></span>

<div id="review_979959166" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/979959166" />
    <a title="Lazaros" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22313662-lazaros"><img alt="Lazaros" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1578697302p2/22313662.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/979959166?book_show_action=true">Jun 28, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lazaros" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lazaros" href="/user/show/22313662-lazaros">Lazaros</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22313662-lazaros?shelf=dystopia">dystopia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22313662-lazaros?shelf=short-stories">short-stories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22313662-lazaros?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22313662-lazaros?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer979959166" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14536596020600238258">I can't help sobbing right now because I just realized that I've read about everything Divergent as of now. <b>I can always re-read the books and novellas but I'm not ever going to read about Tris or Tobias in new adventures.</b> I've loved this characters for so long. I've cherished them for so long. They both hold a place in my heart. It's been a year since I read Allegiant and I'm still sad and stunned about it. With these novellas a chapter just closed, I think. <br/><br/>Tobias is one of the most incredible</span>
  <span id="freeText14536596020600238258" style="display:none">I can't help sobbing right now because I just realized that I've read about everything Divergent as of now. <b>I can always re-read the books and novellas but I'm not ever going to read about Tris or Tobias in new adventures.</b> I've loved this characters for so long. I've cherished them for so long. They both hold a place in my heart. It's been a year since I read Allegiant and I'm still sad and stunned about it. With these novellas a chapter just closed, I think. <br /><br />Tobias is one of the most incredible characters ever written. He's not just tough as nails, he's also sensitive and he's not just loving, he's caring. He is a character with a lot of shit in his past, I think we all know that. Despite that, he didn't let it pull him down. He grew past his problems and he became an amazing human being.<br /><br />In these novellas, we see his progress into being a human. He is hateful in the beginning, he doesn't crack a smile, he doesn't laugh, he doesn't love but we learn that in time he changes into someone with not just a past, but into someone who knows he's got a future. He is not a delusional character, he know who he is, he knows what he is and what he's about. He doesn't just stand by and watch everything go down in flames, he does something about it instead. <br /><br />Just like Allegiant, I loved loved loved the way Mrs. Roth presents us his mind. I love his point of view more than anything. I love his beliefs, and I love who he is and I love the fact that he is not afraid of being afraid. <br /><br />In the last novella, <b>The Traitor</b>, we see how he falls in love. How it's not just beauty that sings to him but also the personality, he falls in love out of the pure emotions that girl, Tris, triggers in him. He doesn't find her gorgeous, he finds her interesting. His first instinct isn't that of protection, he wants to push her until she breaks just so see how brave and tough she is. She is the first person he felt emotions towards to, and by that I don't mean friendly feelings. He learned to love. He and Tris learned to love each other, together. No, no, they didn't learn to love each other, they just loved each other more by loving one another. That's what it took for them to fall in love together, a brush of their hands, a gentle move.. This is love.<br /><br />At some point I'm going to grow so homesick of this series and I'll grab them and read them again because I just can't not love them as much as I do.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14536596020600238258" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1008989361" />
    <a title="Natalie Monroe" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6688207-natalie-monroe"><img alt="Natalie Monroe" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1339730817p2/6688207.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1008989361?book_show_action=true">Jul 28, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Natalie Monroe" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Natalie Monroe" href="/user/show/6688207-natalie-monroe">Natalie Monroe</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Uber Divergent fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6688207-natalie-monroe?shelf=cheesy-cheesy-cheesy">cheesy-cheesy-cheesy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6688207-natalie-monroe?shelf=watch-out-for-puddles-of-angst">watch-out-for-puddles-of-angst</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6688207-natalie-monroe?shelf=when-sparks-don-t-fly">when-sparks-don-t-fly</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1008989361" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7436802263504323077"><blockquote>
  <i>"I look down at her. She has that side, too, she must have it. I saw the way she looked when she beat Molly, like she was going to keep going whether her opponent was unconscious or not. <b>Maybe she and I are the same. </b>"</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>You are, Four, just not in the way you think. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422837484ra/13552425.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>We all remember the disaster that is <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18710190.Allegiant__Divergent___3_' title='Allegiant (Divergent, #3) by Veronica Roth' rel='nofollow noopener'>Allegiant</a>. Tris and Four's voice are totally indistinguishable. Reading a novella entirely in his POV has made me all the more sure. <br/><br/>I don't think it's Roth being unable to write a believable mal</span>
  <span id="freeText7436802263504323077" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>"I look down at her. She has that side, too, she must have it. I saw the way she looked when she beat Molly, like she was going to keep going whether her opponent was unconscious or not. <b>Maybe she and I are the same. </b>"</i>
</blockquote><br><br>You are, Four, just not in the way you think. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422837484ra/13552425.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>We all remember the disaster that is <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18710190.Allegiant__Divergent___3_" title="Allegiant (Divergent, #3) by Veronica Roth" rel="nofollow noopener">Allegiant</a>. Tris and Four's voice are totally indistinguishable. Reading a novella entirely in his POV has made me all the more sure. <br><br>I don't think it's Roth being unable to write a believable male POV. It's a narrative problem; she is incapable of changing style. Of course, we won't know for sure until her untitled duology comes out, but it's my verdict for now. <br><br>What's there to talk about in this collection of short stories? The complete and utter pointlessness. We don't learn anything about Four the original series hasn't told us. He's selfless, a Tris carbon copy, yadda, yadda, yadda. <br><br>We get the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/4502877.Midnight_Sun__Twilight___1_5_" title="Midnight Sun (Twilight, #1.5) by Stephenie Meyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Midnight Sun</a> treatment during romantic scenes between him and Tris. I don't know if it's an Abnegation thing, but his thoughts are far too clean for an 18-year-old boy.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436580609ra/15480335.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Uber Divergent fans will gobble this collection up like cake. For the casual reader, a.k.a me, it's a waste of time.</span>

<div id="review_989857552" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/989857552" />
    <a title="Stepheny" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7091879-stepheny"><img alt="Stepheny" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1567725280p2/7091879.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/989857552?book_show_action=true">Jul 08, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stepheny" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stepheny" href="/user/show/7091879-stepheny">Stepheny</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22021811-four">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer989857552" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5367685445930897685">Yes, I know.<br/><br/>I know what you’re thinking: 3 stars? Really, Stepheny? You? The psychotic Divergent fangirl that turns into a squealing 13 year old every time Four’s name is even mentioned? You’re only giving this 3 stars? <br/><br/>*sigh*<br/><br/>I had to show some extreme self-control in this rating. Part of me wants to give it 5 stars just because. The logical side of me that is trying to look at things objectively says otherwise. <br/><br/>Here are the facts: this book gives us little to no new information. The little bit </span>
  <span id="freeText5367685445930897685" style="display:none">Yes, I know.<br /><br />I know what you’re thinking: 3 stars? Really, Stepheny? You? The psychotic Divergent fangirl that turns into a squealing 13 year old every time Four’s name is even mentioned? You’re only giving this 3 stars? <br /><br />*sigh*<br /><br />I had to show some extreme self-control in this rating. Part of me wants to give it 5 stars just because. The logical side of me that is trying to look at things objectively says otherwise. <br /><br />Here are the facts: this book gives us little to no new information. The little bit of new information we get is great for a fangirl, but just ok for your every day read. I guess I was expecting some more insight into Four’s life <i>prior</i> to him meeting Tris. (You see what I did there, right? Right?) Anyway, we do get a couple stories that show us what his life was like and why he changed factions. But we already kind of knew it. It elaborated points already covered in the Divergent series. And it also gave us snippets of scenes from Divergent but from Four's perspective that made me giggle incessantly. If I've said it once I've said it a hundred times, Roth makes me relive my teenage awkward first love like no other author has done before her. <br /><br />If nothing else, this was an awesome guilty pleasure read! Sometimes you need these types of books just to fill a void you didn’t know you had. <s> Four can fill my void anytime</s> Wait, what? <br /><br /><br /><br />For Divergent junkies like me, you will probably love it. For people who hate the series, avoid it like the plague. For people who enjoy the series and wouldn’t mind a little indulgence- you might enjoy this as well. But just know this: there is nothing new and ground-breaking in this book. It’s strictly entertainment value. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5367685445930897685" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1149320833" />
    <a title="Mariah Roze" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22371819-mariah-roze"><img alt="Mariah Roze" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1496763524p2/22371819.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1149320833?book_show_action=true">Jan 31, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mariah Roze" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mariah Roze" href="/user/show/22371819-mariah-roze">Mariah Roze</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1149320833" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12782334862783855017">It had been an long time since I read the Divergent series, so it is nice getting back into it :)<br/><br/>When reading the Initiate these were the thoughts that were going through my mind. "I really enjoyed this part of the book, Four by Veronica Roth. I do wish there was more development in the extra characters in the story. I wish I knew their histories and backgrounds more, but I understand that Four was an introvert and didn't interact with them much, so it makes since that he wouldn't know this info</span>
  <span id="freeText12782334862783855017" style="display:none">It had been an long time since I read the Divergent series, so it is nice getting back into it :)<br /><br />When reading the Initiate these were the thoughts that were going through my mind. "I really enjoyed this part of the book, Four by Veronica Roth. I do wish there was more development in the extra characters in the story. I wish I knew their histories and backgrounds more, but I understand that Four was an introvert and didn't interact with them much, so it makes since that he wouldn't know this information about them. Also, in Divergent some people did not make the cut, some were hurt outside of the designed fights, some left to become factionless, etc. and in this book none of that happened. I wish a little bit of this would have happened just to keep it even more interesting."<br /><br />When reading The Son these were the thoughts going through my mind. "So before I reviewed the last book/part I should have read this one first. I am so impressed by Veronica's writing ability. Everything that I wish was different because it was "boring" or "simple" had a purpose behind it and was explained in this book. Wow! She is a great writer and this book is very addictive. I like these books way more than 2nd and 3rd books in the trilogy."<br /><br />This was a great book! I loved reading about Tris and Four meeting and getting to know each other from his perspective :) Very cool!<br /><br />I love this story and it was such a nice taste to read a book that I really enjoyed from a different main character's perspective. Authors should write more of these :)<br /><br />I suggest this book to anyone who has read Divergent.</span>

<div id="review_1995218923" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1995218923" />
    <a title="Khurram" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25493797-khurram"><img alt="Khurram" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1383996638p2/25493797.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1995218923?book_show_action=true">May 09, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Khurram" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Khurram" href="/user/show/25493797-khurram">Khurram</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1995218923" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15777901534029524900">Great stories. It was nice to read stories from 4's perspective. The only reason I could not give this 5 stars is because, in Roth's own acknowledgment page, her writing is better through Tris' voice.<br/><br/>Anybody who has read Divergent would know why 4 needed to leave the Abnegation, his trials through Dauntless, to making becoming the legend that is 4. The second, third and fourth story add to work well along side the Divergent book. They show 4's own investigation into the Dauntless conspiracy.<br/><br/>The </span>
  <span id="freeText15777901534029524900" style="display:none">Great stories. It was nice to read stories from 4's perspective. The only reason I could not give this 5 stars is because, in Roth's own acknowledgment page, her writing is better through Tris' voice.<br /><br />Anybody who has read Divergent would know why 4 needed to leave the Abnegation, his trials through Dauntless, to making becoming the legend that is 4. The second, third and fourth story add to work well along side the Divergent book. They show 4's own investigation into the Dauntless conspiracy.<br /><br />The last 3 stories are passages from Divergent rewritten from 4's perspective, they are good, i did like the way way 4 tries to emulate his mentor with the new initiatives. Also the way he puts on a face on for the students but shakes on the inside after a confrontation. Great book a touch below Divergent but still great and and a good compliment to the first book.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15777901534029524900" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2941718817" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2941718817" />
    <a title="♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/52207144"><img alt="♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1568965358p2/52207144.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2941718817?book_show_action=true">Aug 17, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ" href="/user/show/52207144">♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=dystopia-and-utopian">dystopia-and-utopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=novellas">novellas</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2941718817" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18337725352485367691">I always loved Tobias Eaton "<b>Four</b>" in the <i>Divergent</i> series and I always wanted <i>his</i> story. How did I not know this existed? I know, I'm really late to the party but I'm here now, that's what matters right? I really enjoyed reading this and I absolutely love having his POV it was great being inside his head.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1566105674i/28009257._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <u>[0.1] The Transfer ★★★★</u>
</b><br/><b>I have to get out.</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“You’re the one who has to live with your choice. Everyone else will get over it, move on, no matter what you decide. But you never will.” </i>
</b><br/><br/>It wa</span>
  <span id="freeText18337725352485367691" style="display:none">I always loved Tobias Eaton "<b>Four</b>" in the <i>Divergent</i> series and I always wanted <i>his</i> story. How did I not know this existed? I know, I'm really late to the party but I'm here now, that's what matters right? I really enjoyed reading this and I absolutely love having his POV it was great being inside his head.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1566105674i/28009257._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>[0.1] The Transfer ★★★★</u>
</b><br><b>I have to get out.</b><br><br><b>
  <i>“You’re the one who has to live with your choice. Everyone else will get over it, move on, no matter what you decide. But you never will.” </i>
</b><br><br>It was nice getting more back story on Tobias's relationship with his father Marcus too, who may I remind you is a complete POS!!! It was really kinda strange to see such a vulnerable side to him and to see the fear and the struggles he had. I liked seeing this thought process on the whole Choosing Ceremony and how he came to the decision to join Dauntless. Though I do think this was a lot like Tris's story once Tobias joined Dauntless. Wish it would have played out a bit different but nonetheless, it was still interesting. Most of all I loved the bit at the end, finding out how he got his nickname FOUR.❤<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1566103226i/28009201._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>[0.2] The Initiate ★★★★</u>
</b><br><b>I am Dauntless</b><br><br><b>
  <i>“While wounds heal, they don't disappear forever—I carry them everywhere, always, and that is the way of things, the way of scars.”</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>“Abnegation-born, Abnegation result, in a Dauntless haven”</i>
</b><br><br>OH, THIS WAS SOOO GOOD!!! It's even a bit longer than <i>The Transfer</i> which is always a good thing am I right? I can't get enough of <i>Four's</i> POV and I love all this back story. It shows a whole other side to him which makes me love him all the more. Like his initiation and how he trained hard every day and every night he'd go into the fear simulation. I loved glimpsing the struggles he had connecting with others and watching him learn how to interact. It's actually pretty heartbreaking to see. But when your only real interaction is with an abusive father...you have to adjust, and learn how to navigate in this new life (alcohol helps lol). I really love that we got some insight into some other characters that only make an appearance in the <i>Divergent</i> series such as Amar😭, Zeke, and Shauna♡. I really liked Amar's character, he was such a great guy and he generally cares about Four. Such a tragic end. Zeke and Shauna are adorable, I love them! Shauna was cool and I love the whole dynamic with Four teaching her to fight. We also finally get the whole story behind Four and Eric's hostility toward each other. It runs darker than I ever dreamed. Ugh, what a bastard!! I hate Eric so much more now if that were even possible. Anyone up for a little game of DARE? Four gets his first tattoo!<br><br><b>
  <i>“I may have chosen Dauntless as a haven, but I’m not just surviving here, I’m excelling.”</i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1566103226i/28009201._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>[0.3] The Son ★★★</u>
</b><br><b>What I hate, What I love, What I fear</b> <br><br><b>
  <i>“Our city is changing...Sometime soon, everyone will have to choose a side”</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>“That’s what I really want—to shed all the people who want to form and shape me, one by one, and learn instead to form and shape myself.”</i>
</b><br><br><i>The Son</i> was not nearly as good as the first two. It's my least favorite thus far. It was really slow, unexciting, and to be honest, it was very boring. But... it wasn't horrible either. This takes place right after he becomes a Dauntless member and gets his apartment and chooses his career path. This novella includes the moment that Four finds out that his mother <i>Evelyn</i> is still alive. But most importantly it shows that Four found out that Max, Eric, and Jeanine were planning something BIG against Abnegation (which all goes down at the end of Divergent) two years prior. And he does absolutely NOTHING to prevent it. Wow, that's some heroicness right there 😠. This just didn't seem very Four like to me. Oh, and he also acknowledges the fact that Dauntless won't be his home forever. I really really didn't like that it changed my opinion of Four even in the slightest and changed the facts I thought I knew in Divergent and Insurgent.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1566103226i/28009201._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>[0.4] The Traitor ★★★</u>
</b><br><b> Faction before Blood</b><br><br><b>
  <i>“Panic and terror aren't the only kinds of fear. There are deeper kinds, more terrible kinds. Apprehension and heavy, heavy dread.”</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>“I need to talk to someone. I need to trust someone. And for whatever reason, I know, I know it's her.”</i>
</b><br><br><i>The Traitor</i> run parallel to the first part in <i>Divergent</i>. I enjoy reading these novellas from Fours POV but damn... These last two were boring and make Four look/sound weak which contradicts everything he was in the <i>Divergent</i> series. It was nice reading about how Tris and Four met and them getting to know each other but through his eyes. Four struggles with the decision to either betray his faction and warn Abnegation about the upcoming attack or to betray his former faction and tell Abnegation.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1566110692i/28009449._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="18337725352485367691" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_990978820" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Denisse" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8759700-denisse"><img alt="Denisse" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1606102662p2/8759700.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/990978820?book_show_action=true">Jul 09, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Denisse" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Denisse" href="/user/show/8759700-denisse">Denisse</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer990978820" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16933350775845290349"><b>2.5</b> The truth about this is that it is not worth it. I'm sorry. Truth sucks, I know. If you're a fan, go read it! You'll love it.<br/><br/><br/>It's a good move, yhea. -<i>People liked this Divergent thing, the movie made it good enough, lets do some Four-shit thing because we love money. Yes.</i> - It is actually a good move.   <span id="freeText16933350775845290349" style="display:none"><b>2.5</b> The truth about this is that it is not worth it. I'm sorry. Truth sucks, I know. If you're a fan, go read it! The Transfer me lo leí cuando salio y pues nada whatever.         <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1358531270?book_show_action=true">Aug 08, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="- ̗̀meg ̖́-" class="user" itemprop="url" name="- ̗̀meg ̖́-" href="/user/show/32243410---meg--">- ̗̀meg ̖́-</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780007560691" href="/book/show/19530828-four">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32243410---meg--?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1358531270" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7790922052290105854">Actual rating: 4.5 stars<br/><br/>Uhm...wow. I forgot just how much I loved Veronica Roth's writing. This book had been on my tbr pile for months and I'm annoyed at myself for not picking it up sooner. I think that I enjoyed the earlier stories the best (although I do love Tris), the end story and scenes were just extracts of Divergent written from a different PoV. It was awesome to read about Four's character development - he seems like a completely different person in the first story. We, of course, alr</span>
  <span id="freeText7790922052290105854" style="display:none">Actual rating: 4.5 stars<br /><br />Uhm...wow. I forgot just how much I loved Veronica Roth's writing. This book had been on my tbr pile for months and I'm annoyed at myself for not picking it up sooner. I think that I enjoyed the earlier stories the best (although I do love Tris), the end story and scenes were just extracts of Divergent written from a different PoV. It was awesome to read about Four's character development - he seems like a completely different person in the first story. We, of course, already knew about Tobias's background but somehow reading about it in the present tense and in first person really made me understand and like his character a lot more. I'm slightly sad to think that there's no more to come from Veronica, but if she writes anything else I'll be one of the first to read it!</span>
  <a data-text-id="7790922052290105854" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16915293295652531769">When I finished Allegiant, I needed more divergent. But now I need more Four! I LOVED reading this, out of all of my booktubeathon reads so far, this was my favorite. It took me a while to get into divergent at first, so I didn't have high expectations for starting Four, but it was absolutely phenomenal. I only have one complaint: IT WAS WAY TOO SHORT! :)</span>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ICZ3gykvsWiRZvwYoixDCXCyVjyO8K/AQfJnZ+TBpVcE6jgsxT6ROOKzHXXeNZ7amr6myIInu6lFSybB3K7jGg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('CUAym8PutPKvgoLudRpz0Hz+8RhPnDAwGua31wOAapstjH00L/+UotxXY4MJA64DlvIB7ENLJFkeX/ZxO+8s1g==')})
  }
//]]>
